## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (rate laws / concentration-time ODE models)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is explicitly the time-derivative of a species concentration A, which is the standard object modeled by chemical kinetics rate laws. With only (t, A) available, the most likely relationships are autonomous or time-modulated kinetic ODEs expressing consumption/production rates as functions of concentration and possibly explicit time-dependent rate coefficients.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 (constant-rate consumption; surface/photochemical regimes with excess reactant or catalyst saturation)
- First-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A (unimolecular decay, radioactive-like kinetics, many elementary steps under pseudo-first-order conditions)
- Nth-order power-law rate: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical/global rate law where reaction order is fitted)
- Second-order (self-reaction): dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (bimolecular A+A or effective second-order loss)
- Linear relaxation to equilibrium: dA_dt = -c0 * (A - c1) (approach to steady state/equilibrium concentration c1)
- Production + decay balance: dA_dt = c0 - c1 * A (constant inflow/formation with first-order loss; steady state at A = c0/(c1))
- Autocatalytic / logistic-type kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-accelerating growth limited by depletion/carrying capacity-like constraint)
- Saturating (capacity-limited) consumption: dA_dt = -c0 * A / (A + c1) (rate tends to -c0 at large A; mimics saturation by limited catalytic sites/transport)
- Rational inhibition/feedback: dA_dt = -c0 * A / (c1 + c2 * A) (effective rate constant decreases with A due to inhibition or crowding-like effects)
- Time-ramped pseudo-first-order: dA_dt = -(c0 + c1 * t) * A (rate coefficient changes approximately linearly over time due to heating, catalyst activation/deactivation schedule)
- Exponentially varying rate coefficient: dA_dt = -c0 * exp(-c1 * t) * A (decaying driving force such as diminishing illumination, catalyst deactivation, or quencher buildup modeled implicitly in time)
- Periodically forced kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * (c1 + sin(c2 * t)) * A (externally modulated conditions: light on/off, oscillatory feed, periodic mixing effects)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Mass-action structure: if the underlying mechanism is elementary, expect dA_dt proportional to A**n with n near an integer (0, 1, 2), giving straight lines in log(-dA_dt) vs log(A).
- Autonomous vs non-autonomous test: many closed, well-mixed kinetic experiments yield dA_dt = f(A) with no explicit t; explicit t terms often imply changing conditions or missing state variables.
- Sign constraint: for a consumed reactant A (no inflow), dA_dt should be nonpositive for A > 0; fitted models with positive regions often indicate production terms or model misspecification.
- Equilibrium/steady state signature: reversible or buffered systems commonly produce a stable fixed point where dA_dt = 0 at A = c1, captured by a factor (A - c1) or a constant-minus-linear form.
- Saturation/capacity limitation: if rates plateau at high A, prefer hyperbolic/rational dependence in A so dA_dt approaches a finite limit rather than diverging like A**n.
- Autocatalysis fingerprint: rates that are small at very low A, peak at intermediate A, and return toward zero near a limit are well captured by A*(c1 - A).
- Time-dependent rate coefficient clue: if dA_dt at the same A differs systematically across time, include multiplicative modulation by functions of t (linear, exponential, periodic) to represent changing external conditions.

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK1)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A**c1 - c2*A + c3*_w*cos(log(A + c4))
Candidate formulas: 66

GT is the fixed function of **A only** (t does not appear):
\[
f(A)= -0.7725880991\,A^2 -0.7725880991\,A + 0.7402077580\cos(\log(A+1)),
\]
with natural domain \(A>-1\). Key structural requirements for any match (possibly under a domain restriction) are:
- must contain a **quadratic polynomial** term \(\alpha A^2+\beta A\) with \(\alpha=\beta=-0.7725880991\),
- plus an **oscillatory term** exactly \(\gamma\cos(\log(A+1))\) (not \(\sin(A\cdot)\), not \(\cos(A\cdot)\), not \(\cos(\log(kA+1))\) unless it can be made identical to \(\cos(\log(A+1))\)),
- and **no dependence on t** (unless coefficients can be set to 0 to remove t).

Now check candidates.

1. Rational in \(A\) with optional \(\exp(Ac6)\) over \((Ac1+c2)\). No \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). Cannot match.
2. Rational with \(\log(Ac5+1)\) but no cosine of log; also everything divided by \((Ac1+c2)\) so not a polynomial+cos(log) sum. Cannot match.
3. Has \(A c0\), a saturating rational \(A^{c1}c2/(A^{c1}+c3)\), and \(\sin(Ac5+c6)\). Oscillation is in \(A\), not \(\log(A+1)\). Cannot match.
4. Constant + \(\exp(A\cdot)\) + \(\sin(A\cdot)\). Wrong functional forms. Cannot match.
5. Rational with \(\log(Ac6+1)\) terms; no cosine(log). Also divided by linear denom. Cannot match.
6. Includes t-term \(c4 t/(Ac5+c6)\). Even if set \(c4=0\), remaining is linear+exp, no cosine(log). Cannot match.
7. Rational with \(\sin(c5|A|+c6)\) over linear denom. Not \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). Cannot match (even with domain \(A\ge0\), still \(\sin(A)\)-type).
8. Linear + rational + \(\log(Ac5+1)\). No cosine(log). Cannot match.
9. Power \(A^{c0}\) + exp + log + const. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
10. Power + \(\sin(A\cdot)\) + exp + const. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
11. Linear + \(\sin(c2|A|+c3)\) + \(\log(Ac5+1)\). No cosine(log). Cannot match.
12. Linear + \(\log(Ac2+1)\) + \(\sin(A\cdot)\). No cosine(log). Cannot match.
13. Has \(A^2\) and \(A\) and \(\log(Ac4+1)\), but also t-dependent rational term; can set \(c5=c8=0\) to remove t-part, still only log not cos(log). Cannot match.
14. Complicated rational in fractional powers plus log; no cosine(log). Cannot match.
15. \(A^4\) + exp + log + const. Wrong polynomial degree and no cosine(log). Cannot match.
16. Has \(\sin(c2\log(c3|A|+1)+c4)\) which is closer (sin of log), but GT needs **cos(log(A+1))** (no scaling inside log argument except +1, and no absolute). Also has t-dependent rational term removable by setting \(c5=c8=0\). Remaining: \(A c0 + c1\sin(c2\log(c3|A|+1)+c4)\). Problems:
   - only linear in A (no \(A^2\));
   - trig is sin of scaled/shifted log(|A|) not cos(log(A+1)).
   Even with phase shift to convert sin→cos, you still need \(c2=1\), \(c3=1\), and \(|A|\) replaced by \(A\) and domain \(A\ge 0\). But even then it becomes \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) only if \(\log(c3|A|+1)=\log(A+1)\) (requires \(c3=1\) and \(A\ge0\)), and \(c2=1\). That could match the cosine term (via phase), **but there is still no \(A^2\) term**, so cannot match GT.
17. Rational with exp over linear denom. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
18. Rational in \(\sqrt{A}\) etc. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
19. Linear + \(\sin(\log(|A|+1)\cdot)\) + \(\sin(A\cdot)\). Can kill the \(\sin(A\cdot)\) by setting its coefficient 0, and phase-shift sin→cos, and choose domain \(A\ge0\) to drop Abs. Still lacks \(A^2\). Cannot match.
20. Power + exp + t-dependent rational + const. Can remove t-term, still no cosine(log) and no quadratic polynomial necessarily. Cannot match.
21. Linear + \(\sin(|A|)\) + exp. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
22. Rational with exp over linear denom, polynomial degrees 5/4 etc. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
23. Rational + power + exp + const. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
24. Linear + const + \(\sin(A\cdot)\) + exp. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
25. Has rationalized quadratic/linear terms plus \(\sin(A\cdot)\). No cosine(log). Also polynomial part is divided by \((Ac1+1)\) so not a plain polynomial unless \(c1=0\) making denom 1; then you get \(c0A^2+c2A+c6 + c3\sin(Ac4+c5)\). Still trig is \(\sin(A\cdot)\), not \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). Cannot match.
26. If \(c1=0\), becomes \(c0A^2+c2A+c5 + c3\log(Ac4+1)\). Still log, not cos(log). Cannot match.
27. If \(c1=0\), becomes polynomial plus \((A c3 + c7)\sin(Ac4+c5)\). Wrong trig argument. Cannot match.
28. Linear + \(\sin(\log(|A|+1)\cdot)\) + exp. Can remove exp and phase-shift sin→cos and restrict \(A\ge0\), but still no \(A^2\). Cannot match.
29. Power + two exp + const. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
30. Polynomial + exp + log. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
31. Linear + rational + \(\sin(|A|)\). No cosine(log). Cannot match.
32. Polynomial + rational + log. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
33. Linear + rational + \(\sin(\log(|A|+1)\cdot)\). Even if you tune to cos(log(A+1)) under \(A\ge0\), still no \(A^2\) term unless it can come from the rational \(A*c1/(Ac2+c3)\), but that term is at most affine/asymptotic, not exactly quadratic for all A on any interval. Cannot match.
34. Polynomial + \(\sin(A\cdot)\) + log. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
35. Polynomial + two logs. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
36. \(A^5\) + exp + exp + const. Cannot match.
37. Linear + const + \(\sin(A\cdot)\) + log. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
38. Linear + \(\sin(|A|)\) + t-dependent rational. Remove t-term, still no cosine(log) and no \(A^2\). Cannot match.
39. \(A^4\) + \(A^2\) + \(A\) + const + log. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
40. \(A^2\) + \(A\) + \(A^{c2}\) + const + log. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
41. \(A^3\) + \(\sin(A\cdot)\) + exp + const. Cannot match.
42. Linear + rational + saturating rational \(A^{c4}c5/(A^{c4}+c6)\). No cosine(log), and no exact quadratic polynomial. Cannot match.
43. Fractional-power rational. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
44. Linear + rational + const + exp. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
45. Linear + const + log + exp. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
46. Sum of power terms + exp + const. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
47. Linear + \(\sin(c2\log(c3|A|+1)+c4)\) + \(\log(Ac6+1)\). You could phase-shift sin→cos and set \(c2=1,c3=1\) and restrict \(A\ge0\) to get \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). But there is still an extra \(\log(Ac6+1)\) term unless \(c5=0\) (kill it). Then expression is \(A c0 + c1\cos(\log(A+1))\) (after phase). Still missing \(A^2\). Cannot match.
48. If \(c1=0\), becomes \(c0A^2+c2A+c5 + c3\exp(Ac4)\). No cosine(log). Cannot match.
49. Linear + rational + const + log. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
50. Rational + power + const. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
51. Power + const + t-dependent rational. Remove t-term, still no cosine(log) and no fixed quadratic+linear structure. Cannot match.
52. Power + exp(A·) + t-dependent rational. No cosine(log). Cannot match.
53. Power + exp(t) + exp(A). No cosine(log). Cannot match.
54. Rational with \(\sin(c5\log(c6|A|+1)+c7)\) over linear denom. Even if you tune sin-of-log to cos(log(A+1)) under \(A\ge0\) and phase shift, the whole trig term is divided by \((Ac1+c2)\), whereas GT’s cosine term is not multiplied by a rational factor. You could set \(c1=0,c2=1\) to remove the denominator effect, giving \(c0A^2+c3A + (c8+c4A)\sin(\log(A+1)+\phi)+c9\). But then the cosine term would have an unwanted factor \((c8+c4A)\) unless \(c4=0\), leaving constant amplitude OK. Still, you must also match the polynomial part: you can set \(c0=-0.772588...\), \(c3=-0.772588...\), and \(c9=0\). This looks promising except the trig is \(\sin(\log(A+1)+\phi)\) which can be made \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) by choosing \(\phi=-\pi/2\). **However** candidate 54 uses \(\sin(c5\log(c6|A|+1)+c7)\); to get exactly \(\sin(\log(A+1)+\phi)\) you need \(c5=1\), \(c6=1\), and domain \(A\ge0\) to drop Abs. Then with \(c1=0,c2=1,c4=0\), it becomes:
   \[
   c0A^2 + c3A + c8\sin(\log(A+1)+c7) + c9.
   \]
   Set \(c7=-\pi/2\) so \(\sin(\log(A+1)-\pi/2)=-\cos(\log(A+1))\). Then choose \(c8=-0.7402077580\) to get \(+0.7402077580\cos(\log(A+1))\). Set \(c9=0\). This matches GT exactly (on domain \(A\ge 0\), which is a plausible continuous restriction and also within GT’s natural domain \(A>-1\)).
   Therefore candidate 54 **can** be made equivalent under \(A\ge 0\).
55. Power + exp + const + \(\sin(t)\). No.

\[
f(A)= -0.7725880991\,A^2 -0.7725880991\,A + 0.7402077580\cos(\log(A+1)).
\]
Key structural requirements:
- Must contain a **polynomial part** exactly \(\alpha A^2+\beta A\) with \(\alpha=\beta=-0.7725880991\).
- Must contain a **cosine of a logarithm**: \(\gamma\cos(\log(A+1))\) with \(\gamma=0.7402077580\).
- No dependence on \(t\).
- No rational denominators unless they can be made identically 1 on a plausible continuous domain (generally impossible unless the denominator is a constant).

This looks promising—except GT has **no constant offset**, so set \(c9=0\). Then choose \(c2=1\), \(c0=-0.7725880991\), \(c3=-0.7725880991\). For trig: set \(c8=0.7402077580\), \(c5=1\), \(c6=1\), and choose \(c7=\pi/2\) with sine-to-cos conversion: \(\sin(x+\pi/2)=\cos(x)\). Also need Abs removal: restrict domain \(A\ge 0\) (plausible), then \(|A|=A\). Under these settings candidate 54 becomes exactly the GT on \(A\ge 0\). **So 54 matches conditionally.**

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK1)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A**c1 - c2*A + c3*_w*cos(log(A + c4))
Candidates evaluated: 66
Matched candidate IDs: [54]
Matched candidates: ["A**2*c0/(A*c1 + c2) + A*c3/(A*c1 + c2) + A*c4*sin(c5*log(c6*Abs(A) + 1) + c7)/(A*c1 + c2) + c8*sin(c5*log(c6*Abs(A) + 1) + c7)/(A*c1 + c2) + c9/(A*c1 + c2)"]

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.7726*A² - 0.7726*A + 0.7402*cos(log(A + 1))`

The GT has three basis functions: `A²`, `A`, and `cos(log(A+1))`.

Key observations:
- `cos(log(A+1))` is a very specific transcendental function
- No exponential terms in GT
- No `t` dependence in GT

Let me systematically check candidates that could potentially match.

**Candidates with `t` dependence (6, 13, 16, 20, 38, 51, 52, 53, 55, 57, 58, 59, 63, 64, 66):** These can only match if all `t`-dependent terms can be zeroed out. Let me check if the remaining terms could match GT.

**Candidates with `exp` terms (1, 4, 10, 15, 17, 21, 22, 23, 24, 28, 29, 30, 36, 41, 44, 45, 46, 48, 56, 60, 61, 62):** The exp function cannot produce `cos(log(A+1))`, so these need the exp terms zeroed. But then they'd lack the cos(log) term. **NO MATCH** for all of these unless they also have a sin/cos(log) term.

Let me check candidate 28: `A*c0 + c1*sin(c2*log(c3*|A| + 1) + c4) + c5*exp(A*c6)`
- Set c6=0: exp(0)=1, so this becomes `A*c0 + c1*sin(c2*log(c3*|A|+1) + c4) + c5`
- With A≥0, |A|=A. Set c2=1, c3=1, c4=π/2: `sin(log(A+1) + π/2) = cos(log(A+1))`
- This gives: `c0*A + c1*cos(log(A+1)) + c5`
- GT needs A² term. Missing A². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 47:** `A*c0 + c1*sin(c2*log(c3*|A| + 1) + c4) + c5*log(A*c6 + 1)`
- With A≥0: set c2=1, c3=1, c4=π/2 → cos(log(A+1)). But has log(A*c6+1) instead of A². `log` ≠ `A²`. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 19:** `A*c0 + c1*sin(c2*log(c3*|A| + 1) + c4) + c5*sin(A*c6 + c7)`
- Can get cos(log(A+1)) from first sin. But sin(A*c6+c7) cannot produce A². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 16:** `A*c0 + c1*sin(c2*log(c3*|A| + 1) + c4) + c5*t/(A*c6 + c7) + c8/(A*c6 + c7)`
- Zero t terms (c5=0), remaining: `A*c0 + c1*sin(c2*log(c3*A+1)+c4) + c8/(A*c6+c7)`. Missing A². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 33:** `A*c0 + A*c1/(A*c2+c3) + c4*sin(c5*log(c6*|A|+1)+c7) + c8/(A*c2+c3)`
- The rational terms: `A*c0 + (A*c1+c8)/(A*c2+c3)`. This is `A*c0 + (c1/c2) + (c8-c1*c3/c2)/(A*c2+c3)`. Cannot produce A². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 54:** `[A²*c0 + A*c3 + A*c4*sin(c5*log(c6*|A|+1)+c7) + c8*sin(c5*log(c6*|A|+1)+c7) + c9] / (A*c1+c2)`
- Set c1=0, c2=1: `A²*c0 + A*c3 + (A*c4+c8)*sin(c5*log(c6*A+1)+c7) + c9`
- Set c4=0, c5=1, c6=1, c7=π/2: `c0*A² + c3*A + c8*cos(log(A+1)) + c9`
- Set c9=0. This gives: `c0*A² + c3*A + c8*cos(log(A+1))` ✓ **MATCH!**

Let me verify: GT = -0.7726*A² - 0.7726*A + 0.7402*cos(log(A+1)). Yes, this matches with c0=-0.7726, c3=-0.7726, c8=0.7402, c1=0, c2=1, c4=0, c5=1, c6=1, c7=π/2, c9=0.

After checking all remaining candidates similarly, none of the others can produce all three basis functions {A², A, cos(log(A+1))}.
